+  function renderShipments() {
+      const lang = document.documentElement.getAttribute('lang') || 'ar';
+      
+      // Update KPIs
+      const activeCount = shipments.filter(s => s.status === 'transit').length;
+      const warehouseCount = shipments.filter(s => s.status === 'warehouse').length;
+      const deliveredCount = shipments.filter(s => s.status === 'delivered').length;
+      
+      const activeKpi = document.getElementById('kpi-active-count');
+      if (activeKpi) {

+              activeKpiSub.setAttribute('data-en', `${activeCount} active shipments right now`);
+          } else {
+              activeKpiSub.innerText = `${activeCount} active shipments right now`;
+              activeKpiSub.setAttribute('data-ar', `${activeCount} شحنات قيد الحركة حالياً`);

+      }

+      }

+  function openTrackingModal(id) {
+    const ship = shipments.find(s => s.id === id);
+    if (!ship) return;
+
+    const lang = document.documentElement.getAttribute('lang') || 'ar';
+    const modal = document.getElementById('tracking-modal');
+    
+    document.getElementById('track-modal-id').innerText = ship.id;
+    document.getElementById('track-modal-cargo').innerText = lang === 'ar' ? ship.cargo_ar : ship.cargo_en;
+    document.getElementById('track-modal-dest').innerText = lang === 'ar' ? ship.dest_ar : ship.dest_en;
+    
+    const historyList = document.getElementById('track-modal-history');
+    historyList.innerHTML = '';
+    
+    if (ship.history && ship.history.length > 0) {
+      ship.history.slice().reverse().forEach((h, idx) => {
+        const li = document.createElement('div');
+        li.className = `relative pl-8 pb-6 ${idx === 0 ? '' : 'opacity-60'}`;
+        li.innerHTML = `
+          <div class="absolute left-0 top-1 w-3 h-3 rounded-full ${idx === 0 ? 'bg-secondary animate-pulse' : 'bg-outline'} z-10"></div>
+          ${idx !== ship.history.length - 1 ? '<div class="absolute left-[5.5px] top-4 w-px h-full bg-outline-variant"></div>' : ''}
+          <div class="flex flex-col">
+            <span class="text-[10px] font-bold text-on-surface-variant uppercase tracking-wider">${new Date(h.time).toLocaleString(lang === 'ar' ? 'ar-SD' : 'en-US')}</span>
+            <span class="text-xs font-black text-primary mt-1">${lang === 'ar' ? h.location_ar : h.location_en}</span>
+            <p class="text-[11px] text-on-surface-variant mt-0.5">${lang === 'ar' ? h.msg_ar : h.msg_en}</p>
+          </div>
+        `;
+        historyList.appendChild(li);
+      });
+    } else {
+      historyList.innerHTML = `<p class="text-xs text-on-surface-variant italic">${lang === 'ar' ? 'لا يوجد سجل تتبع متاح حالياً لهذه الشحنة.' : 'No tracking history available for this shipment yet.'}</p>`;
     }

+              row.style.opacity = '0';
+              row.style.transform = 'translateX(25px) scale(0.95)';
+          });
       }

+  function createNewShipment(event) {
+    event.preventDefault();
+    
+    const shipId = document.getElementById('form-ship-id').value.trim();
+    const cargo = document.getElementById('form-ship-cargo').value.trim();
+    const dest = document.getElementById('form-ship-dest').value.trim();
+    const status = document.getElementById('form-ship-status').value;
+    const date = document.getElementById('form-ship-date').value.trim();
+
+    const formattedId = shipId.startsWith('#') ? shipId : `#${shipId}`;
+    
+    const lang = document.documentElement.getAttribute('lang') || 'ar';
+    const newShip = {
+        id: formattedId,
+        dest_ar: dest,
+        dest_en: dest,
+        cargo_ar: cargo,
+        cargo_en: cargo,
+        progress: status === 'transit' ? 65 : (status === 'warehouse' ? 30 : 100),
+        status: status,
+        date_ar: date,
+        date_en: date
+    };
+
+    // Add to top
+    shipments.unshift(newShip);
+    renderShipments();
+
+    // Reset Form & Close
+    event.target.reset();
+    closeNewShipmentModal();
+
+    // Trigger Success Notification toast
+    const alertMsg = lang === 'ar' ? 
+        `تم تسجيل الشحنة رقم ${formattedId} بنجاح وإلحاقها بأسطول الملاحة!` : 
+        `Shipment ${formattedId} has been successfully registered and dispatched!`;
+    triggerToastAlert(alertMsg);
+  }

+    function createRouteArc(start, end, color = 0x795900) {
+      const midPoint = new THREE.Vector3().addVectors(start, end).multiplyScalar(0.5);
+      const distance = start.distanceTo(end);
+      midPoint.normalize().multiplyScalar(4 + distance * 0.25);
+      
+      const curve = new THREE.QuadraticBezierCurve3(start, midPoint, end);
+      const points = curve.getPoints(50);
+      const lineGeo = new THREE.BufferGeometry().setFromPoints(points);
+      
+      const lineMat = new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({
+        color: color,
+        transparent: true,
+        opacity: 0.4
+      });
+      
+      return { line: new THREE.Line(lineGeo, lineMat), curve: curve };
+    }
